Doing this could\n207:   /// reduce implementation complexity and avoid potential invalidation\n208:   /// issues that may happen with nested pass managers of the same type.\n209:   template <typename PassT>\n210:   LLVM_ATTRIBUTE_MINSIZE std::enable_if_t<std::is_same_v<PassT, PassManager>>\n211:   addPass(PassT &&Pass) {\n212:     for (auto &P : Pass.Passes)\n213:       Passes.push_back(std::move(P));\n214:   }\n215: \n216:   /// Returns if the pass manager contains any passes.\n217:   bool isEmpty() const { return Passes.empty(); }\n218: \n219:   static bool isRequired() { return true; }\n220: \n221: protected:\n222:   using PassConceptT =\n223:       detail::PassConcept<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>;\n224: \n225:   std::vector<std::unique_ptr<PassConceptT>> Passes;\n226: };\n227: \n228: template <typename IRUnitT>\n229: void printIRUnitNameForStackTrace(raw_ostream &OS, const IRUnitT &IR);\n230: \n231: template <>\n232: LLVM_ABI void printIRUnitNameForStackTrace<Module>(raw_ostream &OS,\n233:                                                    const Module &IR);\n234: \n235: extern template class LLVM_TEMPLATE_ABI PassManager<Module>;\n236: \n237: /// Convenience typedef for a pass manager over modules.\n238: using ModulePassManager = PassManager<Module>;\n239: \n240: template <>\n241: LLVM_ABI void printIRUnitNameForStackTrace<Function>(raw_ostream &OS,\n242:                                                      const Function &IR);\n243: \n244: extern template class LLVM_TEMPLATE_ABI PassManager<Function>;\n245: \n246: /// Convenience typedef for a pass manager over functions.\n247: using FunctionPassManager = PassManager<Function>;\n248: \n249: /// A container for analyses that lazily runs them and caches their\n250: /// results.\n251: ///\n252: /// This class can manage analyses for any IR unit where the address of the IR\n253: /// unit sufficies as its identity.\n254: template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs> class AnalysisManager {\n255: public:\n256:   class Invalidator;\n257: \n258: private:\n259:   // Now that we've defined our invalidator, we can define the concept types.\n260:   using ResultConceptT = detail::AnalysisResultConcept<IRUnitT, Invalidator>;\n261: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d@4152de6435984e9fc55431f4d74a7470d8ac05c0/-/blob/llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManager.h%3FL140-260"}}}

PassManagerInternal.h — Type Erasure Layer\\n\\n`llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManagerInternal.h` defines the abstract base `PassConcept<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>` (virtual `run()` method) and the concrete wrapper `PassModel<IRUnitT, PassT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>`, which implements the type erasure pattern enabling heterogeneous pass storage.\\n\\n### 3. PassManagerImpl.h — Execution Implementation\\n\\n`llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManagerImpl.h` provides the implementation of `PassManager::run()` (line 28). It iterates over the stored passes in sequence, calling `Pass->run(IR, AM, ExtraArgs...)` and using `AM.invalidate(IR, PassPA)` to manage analysis invalidation after each pass.\\n\\n### 4. PassRegistry (Legacy Registration)\\n\\n`llvm/include/llvm/PassRegistry.h` declares the legacy `PassRegistry` class with the singleton `PassRegistry::getPassRegistry()` and `registerPass()` method. The helper template `RegisterPass<T>` in `llvm/include/llvm/PassSupport.h` (line 89) is the idiomatic way to register a legacy IR pass — its constructor calls `PassRegistry::getPassRegistry()->registerPass(*this)`.\\n\\n### 5. New Pass Manager Registry (PassBuilder + PassRegistry.def)\\n\\nFor the new PassManager, passes are registered via the `PassBuilder` class (`llvm/include/llvm/Passes/PassBuilder.h`, `llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilder.cpp`):\\n- `PassBuilder::registerModuleAnalyses(ModuleAnalysisManager &MAM)` iterates over `MODULE_ANALYSIS` entries from `llvm/lib/Passes/PassRegistry.def` and calls `MAM.registerPass(...)` for each.\\n- Similarly for `registerFunctionAnalyses`, `registerCGSCCAnalyses`, `registerLoopAnalyses`.\\n- `llvm/lib/Passes/PassRegistry.def` is the X-macro registry listing all named passes (MODULE_PASS, FUNCTION_PASS, etc.) and analyses (MODULE_ANALYSIS, FUNCTION_ANALYSIS, etc.).\\n- `AnalysisManager::registerPass()` (declared in `llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManager.h`) stores the analysis factory.\\n\\n### 6.
